[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35morg.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander.expand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mExpander.jav[0m[1;92ma:412[0m[1;39m)[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[39mat [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35morg.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander.expand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mExpander.jav[0m[1;92ma:336[0m[1;39m)[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[39mat [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35morg.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander.expand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mExpander.jav[0m[1;92ma:216[0m[1;39m)[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[39mat [0m[1;35mExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1;39m([0m[39mExpanderFuzzer.jav[0m[1;92ma:52[0m[1;39m)[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDEDUP_TOKEN: 7bb3f9683ba8f59b[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m== libFuzzer crashing input ==[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Jazzer fuzzing run against the Apache Commons Compress “Expander” example [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtriggered a `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` exception for file path traversal. The [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzer input caused the library’s expansion logic to attempt writing files outside [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe intended output directory, and the built-in `FilePathTraversal` sanitizer [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdetected and halted this behavior.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue type  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The exception indicates a *file path traversal* vulnerability. The Jazzer [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msanitizer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m flagged [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma critical security issue when it observed that an archive entry’s path would [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mescape the designated output directory.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Stack trace and sanitizer details  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The trace shows the path traversal check failing in [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`com.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.FilePathTraversal`:[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    • `[0m[1;35mcheck[0m[1;39m([0m[39mFilePathTraversal.jav[0m[1;92ma:346[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    • `[0m[1;35mcheckPath[0m[1;39m([0m[39mFilePathTraversal.jav[0m[1;92ma:293[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    • `[0m[1;35mcopyMismatchMvHook[0m[1;39m([0m[39mFilePathTraversal.jav[0m[1;92ma:211[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  These methods are invoked from [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander.expand`, indicating the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerable logic resides in the archive expansion routines.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Fuzzer harness  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The failing input was driven by [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1;39m([0m[39mExpanderFuzzer.jav[0m[1;92ma:52[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. The harness merely [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfeeds bytes to the Expander example; it is not the root cause, but exposes the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39missue by triggering the expansion code path.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Observations  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. The exception originates in the file-path sanitizer rather than native code or[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlow-level I/O.  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. The library’s expansion mechanism attempts to write entries to [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/tmp/[0m[95mexpander-tmp[0m[39m*[0m[35m/output/[0m[95m...[0m[39m`, but an attacker-supplied archive entry manipulates[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe path to break out of the target directory.  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. The DEDUP_TOKEN [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`7bb3f9683ba8f59b`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and “libFuzzer crashing input” message [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfirm a reproducible, unique proof-of-concept file that triggers the sanitizer.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Areas for investigation  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  To gain a holistic view of the issue, review:[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    • `FilePathTraversal` sanitizer class [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmethods `check`, `checkPath`, [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`copyMismatchMvHook`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    • `Expander.expand` overloads in [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander`  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    • The logic that constructs output file paths from archive entry names  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    • Interaction between mismatched copy vs. move operations in the expander  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    • Any utility methods that normalize or sanitize entry names before filesystem [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperations  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNo assumptions are made about root causes or fixes; this report strictly documents [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe observed behavior, vulnerability type, and relevant code areas for further [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39manalysis.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Centralize and strengthen path‐sanitization in the `Expander` example  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Introduce a private helper in `Expander.java`:  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[39m**[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       * Resolve an archive entry name against the target directory,[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       * normalize the result, and prevent path traversal.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      private static Path [0m[1;35mresolveInDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath baseDir, String entryName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIOException [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          Path resolved = [0m[1;35mbaseDir.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mentryName[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mresolved.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbaseDir[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mString.format[0m[1;39m([0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  [0m[32m"Zip slip '%s' + '%s' -> '%s'"[0m[39m, baseDir, entryName, resolved[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          return resolved;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. In the ZIP‐specific `[0m[1;35mexpand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mZipFile archive, Path targetDirectory[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39maround lines [0m[1;36m470[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m505[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, replace all manual `[0m[1;35mresolve[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` + [0m            [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      – Symlink branch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m480[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m489[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        • Change[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```java[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          Path link = [0m[1;35mtargetDirectory.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mzae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          Path target = [0m[1;35mtargetDirectory.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m existing parent‐creation + symlink logic[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          to[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```java[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          Path link = [0m[1;35mresolveInDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirectory, [0m[1;35mzae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          Path target = [0m[1;35mresolveInDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirectory, targetName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        • Remove any additional ad hoc parent‐relativize logic that attempts to [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“fix” paths; rely on `resolveInDirectory` to catch traversal.  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      – File branch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m490[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m505[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        • Change[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```java[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          Path target = [0m[1;35mtargetDirectory.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mzae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mtarget.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirectory[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m throw … [0m[1;39m}[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          to[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```java[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          Path target = [0m[1;35mresolveInDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirectory, [0m[1;35mzae.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        • Leave the parent‐creation [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mcreateParentDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirectory, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtarget[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and `[0m[1;35mFiles.copy[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` in place—but remove the extra “parent mismatch” [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mblock [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m497[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m500[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m since our helper already enforces correct parentage.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Extend the same helper to any other specialized `[0m[1;35mexpand[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` overloads  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – If there are CP/M, TAR‐stream, or other format overloads in `Expander`, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrefactor their path‐resolution blocks to invoke `resolveInDirectory` before [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcreating directories or opening streams.  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Preserve the generic `[0m[1;35mexpand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mArchiveEntrySupplier, ArchiveEntryBiConsumer, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – It already uses `ArchiveEntry.resolveIn`, which applies the same [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnormalize+startsWith guard. No changes needed here—tests for non‐ZIP formats remain[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munaffected.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Rationale and benefits  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Uniformly centralizes traversal checks, eliminating duplication and subtle [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minconsistencies between ZIP and other formats.  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – By throwing a checked `IOException` at resolution time, we prevent any [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdownstream file‐system calls on illegal paths, stopping the sanitizer from firing [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand avoiding partial extraction.  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Valid entries [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno “..[0m[35m/[0m[39m” or absolute names[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m map to the same paths as before; no[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisting non‐malicious use cases are broken.  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – The fix does not touch fuzz harnesses, test code, or external [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdependencies—compliant with patch guidelines.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Mitigations and side‐effects  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Consumers may now see an immediate `IOException` for traversal attempts rather[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthan a sanitizer‐driven crash. This is acceptable for an example program and safer [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mby design.  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – No broad exception catching is introduced; only the specific resolution step [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthrows.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Existing unit and integration tests for `Expander` that expect successful [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextraction of valid archives will continue passing without modification.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/examples/Expander.jav[0m[1;92ma:508[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m524[0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The compilation errors [0m[1;39m([0m[39m“class, interface, or enum expected”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m indicate that [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe helper method `createParentDirectory` and its body are no longer inside the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Expander` class due to a stray closing brace [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m inserted after the `expand` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethod.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The last patch added three consecutive closing braces at the end of `expand` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mone too many[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which prematurely closes the class body. As a result, everything [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfollowing that extra brace is treated as top‐level code, triggering syntax errors.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Critical Logic to Preserve  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The newly introduced helper `[0m[1;35mresolveInDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath, String[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` must remain as [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma private static method inside the `Expander` class.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The modified `expand` method’s calls to `resolveInDirectory` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mreplacing manual[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnormalization and `startsWith` checks[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are the intended security fix and must be [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mretained.  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The existing `createParentDirectory` helper and all other functionality must [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremain intact and inside the class.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Fix Steps  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Open [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/examples/Expander.java`.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Locate the end of the `[0m[1;35mexpand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mZipFile, Path[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method. You will see three [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclosing braces in a row, for example:  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Remove the extra middle `[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe one introduced by the last patch[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. After [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremoval, you should have exactly two braces closing `[0m[1;35mwhile[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and then [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mexpand[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, like so:  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Verify that immediately after those two braces, the declaration of  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      `private static Path [0m[1;35mcreateParentDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath root, Path target[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` appears [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mat the same indent level as `public void [0m[1;35mexpand[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and `private static Path [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mresolveInDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. This ensures all three methods reside within the class.  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   e. Confirm that there is still one final `[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m` at the very end of the file that [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcloses the `Expander` class.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Validation  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Rebuild the project [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`mvn compile` or your standard build command[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to ensure [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mno “class, interface, or enum expected” errors remain.  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run existing unit tests and fuzz harnesses to verify that extraction [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctionality and path‐slip checks remain operational.  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Specifically validate that:  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Normal file entries and Unix symlinks continue to be extracted under [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`targetDirectory`.  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Attempts to traverse outside `targetDirectory` [0m[1;39m([0m[39musing `..[0m[35m/[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throw an [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`IOException` from `resolveInDirectory`.  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification and Side‐Effect Mitigation  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By only removing the extra brace, we restore the correct class/method [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstructure without altering any logic or external APIs.  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The security improvement from the helper method is untouched; manual [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnormalization code has already been replaced.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No harness code, tests, or utility functions outside `Expander.java` are [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmodified, so existing tests and fuzzers will continue to pass unchanged.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If further brace‐related issues appear, count opening vs. closing braces in [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe class to ensure they match.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis repair re‐establishes proper Java syntax, keeps the security patch intact, and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mavoids unintended changes to surrounding functionality.  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         # Evaluation Report                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         The initial issue arises when running a Jazzer-based fuzzer against the Apache      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Commons Compress `Expander` example. The fuzzer triggers a                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` exception reporting a file path traversal             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         vulnerability [1m([0m`[35m/tmp/[0m[95mexpander-[0m…[35m/[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m`[1m)[0m. In response, a patch was        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         applied that removed a closing brace in `Expander.java`, intending to keep helper   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         methods inside the class. After applying that change, the build fails with a Java   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         compilation error [1m([0m`illegal start of expression`[1m)[0m in `Expander.java`.               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m. Initial Issue                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - A Jazzer fuzzing run on `ExpanderFuzzer` aborts with:                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              ```                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: File path        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         traversal: [35m/tmp/.../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                at [1;35mFilePathTraversal.check[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                at [1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                …                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              ```                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - This indicates that the fuzzer triggered the path-traversal sanitizer in       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `FilePathTraversal.copyMismatchMvHook`, invoked by `Expander.expand`.               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m. Important Observations                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The exception is generated by the Jazzer sanitizer, not by Java’s standard     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         exception hierarchy.                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The stack trace pins the issue to calls within                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander`.                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The harness [1m([0m`ExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[1m)[0m exercises the `Expander`     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         logic with arbitrary archive inputs, making it clear that untrusted archive entries [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         can escape intended extraction roots.                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m. Patch Attempt                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - A single-line patch was applied to `Expander.java`:                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              ```diff                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              -    [1m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              +[35m/[0m[35m/[0m removed stray closing brace to keep helper methods inside the class        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              ```                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The removed `[1m}[0m` was located just after a nested block ending at line [1;36m502[0m of    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `Expander.java`.                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The intention appeared to be to merge helper methods [1m([0msuch as                  [2m                [0m
